    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[Code], [c].[CountyId], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedBy], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[Name], [c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[UpdatedBy]
    FROM [Constituencies] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t1] ON [t0].[ConstituencyId] = [t1].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[Code], [c0].[CreatedAt], [c0].[CreatedBy], [c0].[IsDeleted], [c0].[Name], [c0].[UpdatedAt], [c0].[UpdatedBy]
    FROM [Counties] AS [c0]
    WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t2] ON [t1].[CountyId] = [t2].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[Code], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedBy], [c1].[DepartmentId], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[Name], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [c1].[UpdatedBy]
    FROM [Clusters] AS [c1]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t3] ON [t].[ClusterId] = [t3].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [t].[ProjectLeadId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[AssignedAt], [p0].[CreatedAt], [p0].[CreatedBy], [p0].[IsDeleted], [p0].[ProjectId], [p0].[RevokedAt], [p0].[Role], [p0].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[UpdatedBy], [p0].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[AccessFailedCount], [u0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [u0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [u0].[Email], [u0].[EmailConfirmed], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[IsActive], [u0].[LastLoginAt], [u0].[LastName], [u0].[LockoutEnabled], [u0].[LockoutEnd], [u0].[NormalizedEmail], [u0].[NormalizedUserName], [u0].[PasswordHash], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [u0].[SecurityStamp], [u0].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u0].[UserName], [u0].[BaseLatitude], [u0].[BaseLongitude], [u0].[BaseRadiusInMeters]
    FROM [ProjectAssignments] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u0] ON [p0].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
    WHERE [p0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t4] ON [t].[Id] = [t4].[ProjectId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [w0].[Id], [w0].[CreatedAt], [w0].[CreatedBy], [w0].[Description], [w0].[FilePath], [w0].[IsDeleted], [w0].[IsGeoValidated], [w0].[Progress], [w0].[ProjectId], [w0].[Title], [w0].[UpdatedAt], [w0].[UpdatedBy], [w0].[SubmissionLatitude], [w0].[SubmissionLongitude], [w0].[SubmissionRadiusInMeters]
    FROM [WeeklyReports] AS [w0]
    WHERE [w0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t5] ON [t].[Id] = [t5].[ProjectId]
ORDER BY [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id], [t2].[Id], [t3].[Id], [u].[Id], [t4].[Id], [t4].[Id0]
